#masthead -->\n\n\t<div id=\"content\" class=\"site-content\">\n\n\t\t<div class=\"top-section\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t<div class=\"container main-content-area\">\n            \t\t\t<div class=\"row pull-left\">\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"main-content-inner col-sm-12 col-md-8\">\n\n\t<div id=\"primary\" class=\"content-area\">\n\t\t<main id=\"main\" class=\"site-main\" role=\"main\">\n\n\t\t\n<article id=\"post-61261\" class=\"post-61261 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-other-writers tag-bishop-williamson tag-brbara-spectre tag-migrant-crisis\">\n\t\t<div class=\"post-inner-content\">\n\t\t<header class=\"entry-header page-header\">\n\n\t\t\t<h1 class=\"entry-title \">Who is to blame for the Migrant Crisis in Europe?</h1>\n\n\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"byline\"> <i class=\"fa fa-user fa-2x\"></i> <span class=\"author vcard\"><a class=\"url fn n\" href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/author/admin/\">Admin</a></span></span><span class=\"posted-on\"><i class=\"fa fa-calendar\"></i> <a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/who-is-to-blame-for-the-migrant-crisis-in-europe/\" rel=\"bookmark\"><time class=\"entry-date published\" datetime=\"2017-03-01T06:00:00+00:00\">March 1, 2017</time><time class=\"updated\" datetime=\"2017-03-01T00:42:51+00:00\">March 1, 2017</time></a></span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"cat-links\"><i class=\"fa fa-folder-open-o\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t\t <a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/category/other-writers/\" rel=\"category tag\">Other Writers</a>\t\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t</div><!-- .entry-meta -->\n\t\t</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\n\t\t<div class=\"entry-content\">\n\t\t\t<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><strong>By <a href=\"https://mail.google.com/mail/ca/u/0/#inbox/15a7a89ce02c4787\"><em>BISHOP RICHARD WILLIAMSON</em></a></strong></p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">&#8220;White European males abandon God?<br/>\nBlacks, Muslims, females, Jews serve as His rod!&#8221;</h4>\n<p><strong>So there is a Global Power behind the on-going flood of non-European immigrants into Europe, and religion is \u201cdecisive\u201d in that flood \u2013 so said last week\u2019s \u201cEleison Comments.\u201d Then two questions arise \u2013 who or what is that power? And how can religion enter into such a political question?</strong><span id=\"more-61261\"></span></p>\n<h6><img class=\"alignleft size-medium wp-image-61263\" src=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/xwilliamson-225x300.jpg.pagespeed.ic.iLr2yW4_yp.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"225\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/williamson-225x300.jpg 225w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/williamson-113x150.jpg 113w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/williamson.jpg 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 225px) 100vw, 225px\"/>His Excellency Bishop Richard Williamson <em>(pictured)</em></h6>\n<p>As to the identity of that Global Power, of whose existence the Hungarian economist was so sure without his ever being willing to identify it, there is easily accessible on the Internet (unless it has been smothered) a fascinating and frightening clip from an interview filmed in 2010, only a few minutes long, in which a Jewess claims that it is the Jews who are leading the multi-cultural transformation of Europe.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barbara_Lerner_Spectre\"><strong>Barbara Spectre</strong></a> was born in the USA in 1942, graduated in philosophical studies in the USA, was active as a professional educator from 1967 in Israel, and in1999 emigrated to Sweden to join her husband who was Rabbi there of the Stockholm Synagogue.</p>\n<p>If one watches the clip [at the end of this article], it seems evident that nobody is forcing her to reveal who is behind the transformation of Europe now taking place.</p>\n<p>Rather she sincerely believes in that transformation and in what the Jews are doing to Europe, because she claims that the immigrant invasion will alone enable Europe to survive.</p>\n<p>Here are her own words:</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-61262\" src=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/wpid-barbara-spectre-quote.jpg.pagespeed.ce.RlAb7i-t5s.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"640\" height=\"524\" srcset=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/wpid-barbara-spectre-quote.jpg 640w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/wpid-barbara-spectre-quote-150x123.jpg 150w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/wpid-barbara-spectre-quote-300x246.jpg 300w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/wpid-barbara-spectre-quote-600x491.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 640px) 100vw, 640px\"/></p>\n<p>Here is a convincing answer to the question of the identity of the Global Power.</p>\n<blockquote><p><strong>Active at university level for over 30 years in Israel, ardent Zionist and wife of a Rabbi, Barbara Spectre could easily know what Jews were planning for Europe, years before the immigrant invasion of Europe became today\u2019s flood. </strong></p></blockquote>\n<p>And Jewish mastery of all five elements named by the Hungarian economist as being necessary to set up a flood of immigrants makes the identification of his \u201cGlobal Power\u201d with Jewish power entirely plausible.</p>\n<p>But why would Jews want to turn \u201cmonolithic\u201d Europe into \u201cmulti-culti\u201d Europe? The answer is a driving force that goes far behind and above mere politics.</p>\n<p>Ever since the Pharisees and Scribes crucified Our Lord Jesus Christ because he was turning God\u2019s people from theirs by race into His by Catholic faith, they have persecuted His Church for nearly two millennia (read Maurice Pinay\u2019s <strong><a href=\"https://christogenea.org/system/files/resources/PlotAgainstTheChurchComplete.pdf\">The Plot Against the Church</a></strong> ).</p>\n<h3>Still today Jewish leaders believe in their unique God-given gifts and rights to govern the world.</h3>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-61264\" src=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/96dac860fcfab6fa8779bd7ab6c5396b.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"449\" height=\"450\" srcset=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/96dac860fcfab6fa8779bd7ab6c5396b.jpg 449w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/96dac860fcfab6fa8779bd7ab6c5396b-150x150.jpg 150w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/96dac860fcfab6fa8779bd7ab6c5396b-300x300.jpg 300w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/96dac860fcfab6fa8779bd7ab6c5396b-60x60.jpg 60w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 449px) 100vw, 449px\"/></p>\n<p><strong>Now the Old Testament did come from God, but it points straight to the New Testament which replaced it, and so the successors of the Pharisees had to twist the Old Testament into the Talmud, which is viciously anti-Christian. Therefore Talmudism is a false religion, but it has given pseudo-religious backing and power to the age-old Pharisaic drive to kill off Christianity.</strong></p>\n<p>Now Christ\u2019s Church was born and bred in the Middle East, and spread rapidly all around the Mediterranean Sea, but when the Middle East and North Africa fell to Islam, then the Faith was upheld and spread world-wide mainly by Europeans, of the white race, and divided by Providence into the variety of European nations.</p>\n<p>Thus St Francis Xavier in India begged St Ignatius to send to him European priests from Europe to act as missionaries. Hence the quasi-religious hatred of the Pharisees\u2019 successors for the white nations of Europe, and hence the Jews\u2019 \u201cmulti-culti\u201d drive to dilute that white race and dissolve the \u201cmonolithic\u201d nations of Europe.</p>\n<p>Unless these nations turn back to God and His one true Church, His Justice risks allowing that drive to succeed, unless His Mercy interrupts it\u00a0.\u00a0.\u00a0.</p>\n<p><em>Kyrie eleison.</em></p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"color: #800000;\">VIDEO (37 seconds)</span></h4>\n<p><iframe width=\"648\" height=\"365\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/8ERmOpZrKtw?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>\n<!-- Simple Share Buttons Adder (6.3.4) simplesharebuttons.com --><div class=\"ssba ssba-wrap\"><div style=\"text-align:center\">Like this? \ud83d\ude42</p>\n<p><strong>Trump is going to Italy in May, so will he meet the pope?</strong></p>\n<p>In\u00e9s San Mart\u00edn<br/>\nFebruary 6, 2017<br/>\nVATICAN CORRESPONDENT </p>\n<p>ROME-The White House announced on Sunday that President Donald Trump will be travelling to Italy to attend a G7 summit in May, and some believe this might be an opportunity for him to meet with Pope Francis.</p>\n<p>The possibility of the two leaders\u2019 first meet-and-greet was first suggested by Christopher Lamb in The Tablet, who quoted a diplomatic source saying that if Trump came to Italy without seeing the pope, it would be seen as \u201ca snub, particularly given their earlier clashes over migration.\u201d</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://cruxnow.com/vatican/2017/02/06/trump-going-italy-may-will-meet-pope/\" rel=\"nofollow\">https://cruxnow.com/vatican/2017/02/06/trump-going-italy-may-will-meet-pope/</a></p>\n<p>\u2026\u2026\u2026\u2026\u2026\u2026\u2026\u2026\u2026\u2026\u2026\u2026.</p>\n<p>John L. class=\"comment-author vcard\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<img alt='' src='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/028c9ed93d3715863a09bb6a468f6cdf?s=60&#038;d=mm&#038;r=pg' href='http://Conspiracyofman.com' rel='external nofollow' class='url'>Arch Stanton</a></b> <span class=\"says\">says:</span>\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-author -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-metadata\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/who-is-to-blame-for-the-migrant-crisis-in-europe/#comment-948234\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<time datetime=\"2017-03-01T17:48:57+00:00\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tMarch 1, 2017 at 5:48 pm\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</time>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-metadata -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</footer><!-- .comment-meta -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<blockquote><p>Now the Old Testament did come from God, but it points straight to the New Testament which replaced it, and so the successors of the Pharisees had to twist the Old Testament into the Talmud, which is viciously anti-Christian. Therefore Talmudism is a false religion, but it has given pseudo-religious backing and power to the age-old Pharisaic drive to kill off Christianity.</p></blockquote>\n<p>All three religions, whore Judaism and her two horrid daughters, are &#8220;false&#8221; religions.</p>\n<p>Most assuredly the Old Testament came from a &#8220;god,&#8221; but what or who was this &#8220;god?&#8221; The priest was the god of the Old Testament. This explains why that god exhibits the usual human characteristics of judgement, greed, anger, fear, and hatred.  </p>\n<p>The voice of the Old Testament god emanated from the priests. While not officially identified as such, Moses was the first of such priests that delivered &#8220;god&#8217;s&#8221; word to the masses. Most notably, Melchizedek, the high priest of Salem was obviously &#8220;god&#8217;s&#8221; brain behind Abram. This is made evident in the story of the war against Chedorlaomer at Siddim Vale by the fact Abram sacrificed ten percent of his war booty to this priest/god that came out of nowhere. </p>\n<p>The god of the Old Testament was a false god that poisoned the Jews then, and whose false teachings still poisons Jews today, along with those who believe in Judaism&#8217;s religious offshoots. Jesus was the antidote to the priests&#8217; Old Testament poison as Matthew 23 points out in no uncertain terms. </p>\n<p>However, in his effort to undermine the bloody sacrificial system oppressing first century Jews, Jesus had to work within the religious system. For this reason, he claimed legal right to the Old Testament god and his teachings. Jesus said, &#8220;I have come to fulfill the law.&#8221; Thus he came to end Old Testament law vastly enriching the Temple and its priesthood while impoverishing the religious followers supporting its system. </p>\n<p>The Gospels are thus antithetical to, not supportive of, the Old Testament and its laws. This point is made clear when Jesus supersedes all Old Testament law with his two laws. The first law \u201cYou shall love the Lord your God with all your heart and with all your soul and with all your mind. This is the great and first commandment.&#8221; The second law is: &#8220;You shall love your neighbor as yourself.&#8221; All other religious law rest on these two commandments. </p>\n<p>Nothing has changed. Saul simply rehashed the Old Testament, making Jesus its new god. Then later Christians used Saul&#8217;s message to build their new Temple, the Catholic church, continuing Saul&#8217;s tradition of using Jesus as its new god. Jesus would have been appalled by these developments. One only needs look at his words and actions to see this is the case. Jesus talks about destroying the second Temple, yet where does he speak its building a replacement?</p>\n<p>Today Talmudvision priests are still presenting themselves as god&#8217;s official mouth piece and administrators, greatly enriching themselves in the process. </p>\n<p>&#8220;The lower classes of society are those who fatten themselves in the name of religion.&#8221; &#8211; Ibin el-Mubarak</p>\n<p>Here are a few ancient thoughts on religion and those that follow them. Note that Jesus is said to &#8220;stand, in a sense, at the head of the Sufis.&#8221;</p>\n<p>Miracles and Tricks &#8211;<br/>\nBahaudin once received a mendicant Qalander who offered to perform miracles to prove that he was a representative of the greatest of all mystical masters.</p>\n<p>El Shah said:<br/>\n&#8216;We here in Bokhara the unique community whose faith is neither produced nor sustained, in the smallest particular by extraordinary happenings called miracles. But it is of value for you to perform before the whole assembly of dervishes and also all those who come to see us.&#8217;</p>\n<p>He accordingly arranged for the next festival day to be set aside for the performance of the strange Qualander.</p>\n<p>For a whole day, the mendicant performed miracle after miracle: he brought the dead back to life, he walked on water, he caused a severed head to speak, and many other wonders.</p>\n<p>The Bokharans were in an uproar. Some of them stated that this man must be a disciple of the devil, for they did not want to adopt his way of life or to credit him with any beneficent powers. Some of the peripheral supporters of El-Shah declared themselves to be satisfied that &#8216;a new Sun had arisen&#8217;, and tried to make arrangements to leave for wherever his monastery might be. Some of the newer disciples of El-Shah begged him to perform similar miracles, to show the he was capable of them.</p>\n<p>Bahaudin did nothing for three days. Then before an immense concourse of people, he started to perform what can only be called miracles. One after another, people saw things which they could hardly  believe. They saw, heard and touched such things as were not even imagined in the traditions about the wonders of the greatest saints of all time. Then Bahaudin, one after another, showed them how the tricks were carried out, and that they were &#8211; tricks.</p>\n<p>&#8216;Those of you who are seekers of juggling &#8211; follow the way of the juggler,&#8217; he said, &#8216;for I am at more serious work.'&#8221;      </p>\n<p>To be a believer &#8211;<br/>\nYou probably seem to yourself to be a believer, even if you are a believer in disbelief.<br/>\nBut you cannot really believe in anything until you are aware of the process by which you arrived at your position.</p>\n<p>Before you do this you must be ready to postulate that all your beliefs my be wrong, that what you think to be belief may only be a variety of prejudice caused by your surroundings &#8211; including the bequest of your ancestors for whom you may have sentiment.</p>\n<p>True belief belongs to the realm of real knowledge.</p>\n<p>Until you have knowledge, belief is is mere coalesced opinions, however it may seem to you.<br/>\nCoalesced opinions serve for ordinary living. Real belief enables higher studies to be made. &#8211; Attributed to Ali</p>\n<p>On faith and religion &#8211;<br/>\nThose who are regarded as believers or religious people and who are incapable because of habit from behaving in any other manner, may be called religious but cannot be regarded  as having faith. If, on the other hand, this is faith, then some other word should be used to convey the kind of faith which is not produced by the parents or surroundings of a person.   </p>\n<p>What must come &#8211;<br/>\nTo those who seek truth in conventional religion:<br/>\nUntil college and minaret have crumbled<br/>\nThis holy work of ours will not be done.<br/>\nUntil faith becomes rejection<br/>\nAnd rejection becomes belief<br/>\nThere will be no true believer.</p>\n<p>Worship &#8211;<br/>\nO Lord!<br/>\nIf I worship you from fear of hell cast me into hell.<br/>\nIf I worship you from desire for paradise, deny me paradise. &#8211; Rabia el-Adawia</p>\n<p>Service &#8211;<br/>\nI will not serve god like a labourer, in expectation of my wages &#8211; Rabia el-Adawia</p>\n<p>Emptiness &#8211;<br/>\nEveryone in the ordinary world is asleep. Their religion &#8211; the religion of the familiar world &#8211; is emptiness, not religion at all &#8211; Sanai, <i>Hadiqa</i></p>\n<p>The being of God &#8211;<br/>\nNo human mind can attain an understanding of the form of being which is called &#8220;god.&#8221;</p>\n<p>When Hasan of Basra was asked: &#8216;What is Islam, and who are the Muslims?&#8217; He answered:<br/>\n&#8216;Islam is in the books and Muslims are in the tomb.&#8217;</p>\n\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-content -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"reply\"><a rel='nofollow' class='comment-reply-link' Any references to Nicky Rockefeller&#8217;s father teaching in Beijing?</p>\n\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-content -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</article><!-- .comment-body -->\n</li><!-- #comment-## -->\n</ol><!-- .children -->\n</li><!-- #comment-## -->\n\t\t<li id=\"comment-948327\" class=\"comment odd alt depth-2 parent\">\n\t\t\t<article id=\"div-comment-948327\" class=\"comment-body\">\n\t\t\t\t<footer class=\"comment-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-author vcard\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<img alt='' src='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/44949a80a6e3af20b81db86f165130bc?s=60&#038;d=mm&#038;r=pg' srcset='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/44949a80a6e3af20b81db86f165130bc?s=120&amp;d=mm&amp;r=pg 2x' class='avatar avatar-60 photo' height='60' width='60'/>\t\t\t\t\t\t<b class=\"fn\">Pat</b> <span class=\"says\">says:</span>\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-author -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-metadata\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/who-is-to-blame-for-the-migrant-crisis-in-europe/#comment-948327\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<time datetime=\"2017-03-02T22:11:28+00:00\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tMarch 2, 2017 at 10:11 pm\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</time>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-metadata -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</footer><!-- .comment-meta -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p>Winston &#8211;</p>\n<p>Nothing on Nick&#8217;s dad and China.</p>\n<p>You wrote:</p>\n<p>&#8220;What is undeniable is that Russia paid off her debt.&#8221;</p>\n<p>I found that the closest to Russia paying off the debt of the Central bank was the paying down of 17% of the debt in 2014. </p>\n<p>Putin might have paid off Rothschild for what he owed him on one of his elaborate mansions.. \ud83d\ude42</p>\n<p>Russia issues debt. Bonds. They boast having ONE OF the lowest GOVERNMENT DEBT in the world&#8230;. but nowhere near zero.</p>\n<p>Russia is a debt-based economy.</p>\n<p>&#8230;&#8230;</p>\n<p><strong>Ksenia Yudaeva: National debt &#8211; vice or virtue?</strong></p>\n<p>Statement by Ms Ksenia Yudaeva, Deputy Governor of the Bank of Russia, at the Gaidar Forum 2016 &#8220;Russian and the world &#8211; looking to the future&#8221;, panel discussion &#8220;National debt &#8211; vice or virtue?&#8221;, Moscow, 13 January 2016.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.bis.org/review/r160118a.htm\" rel=\"nofollow\">https://www.bis.org/review/r160118a.htm</a> </p>\n<p>(excerpts)</p>\n<p><strong>Does Russia have a\u00a0potential to\u00a0build up\u00a0government debt?<br/>\nYes, it\u00a0does, in theory, since our country may boast one of\u00a0the lowest levels of\u00a0government debt.</strong></p>\n<p><strong>&#8212;Consequently, the development of\u00a0the government debt market could be conducive to\u00a0the development of\u00a0the financial system as\u00a0a\u00a0whole.&#8212;</strong> </p>\n<p>Anyway I\u00a0would proceed from the conservative assessments of\u00a0the maximum possible debt burden on\u00a0the Russian economy, which does not pose a\u00a0threat to\u00a0macroeconomic stability, say, no\u00a0more than 25-30% of\u00a0GDP. Anyway examples from the Russian history show that the real interest rates the Russian budget has to\u00a0pay, should the government debt exceed 35-40%, became exorbitant and accelerated the debt spiral. </p>\n<p>Among the negative outcome of\u00a0government debt growth\u00a0I may also call the ousting of\u00a0corporate and private borrowers by\u00a0the state. </p>\n<p><strong>By\u00a0the way, the maximum permissible debt burden is\u00a0higher in\u00a0the countries witnessing persistently low inflation and persistently low inflation expectations. The long-term real interest rates in\u00a0these countries are lower, which means that debt burden limits are higher.</strong> This is\u00a0another manifestation of\u00a0interdependence between fiscal and monetary policies: the more successful the central bank is\u00a0in\u00a0terms of\u00a0securing sustainable price stability, the larger is\u00a0the room for manoeuvre used by\u00a0the Government to\u00a0build up\u00a0budget deficit and government debt to\u00a0pursue a\u00a0countercyclical policy.</p>\n<p><strong>Actually, there is\u00a0no\u00a0choice whether the government debt is\u00a0good or\u00a0bad.</strong></p>\n<p> Any medicine can be\u00a0fatal, or\u00a0at\u00a0least toxic, if\u00a0overdosed. The same is\u00a0true of\u00a0the government debt: it\u00a0can easily turn out from a\u00a0basis for the financial system development to\u00a0its grave digger. This is\u00a0one of\u00a0the reasons which cannot help being taken into account in\u00a0shaping fiscal policy.</p>\n<p>Whether the government debt is\u00a0good or\u00a0bad, as\u00a0I have already mentioned, is\u00a0a\u00a0sham question to\u00a0a\u00a0certain extent. </p>\n<p><strong>An important question is\u00a0how to\u00a0finance the deficit: through reserves or through debt?</strong> </p>\n<p>Strictly speaking, both options lead to\u00a0growth in\u00a0net debt (net of\u00a0reserves) and consequently to\u00a0debt burden accumulation. That is\u00a0why this choice is\u00a0also a\u00a0sham one to\u00a0a\u00a0large extent. Nevertheless, since the commodity market risks are high, we\u00a0believe that today the priority should be\u00a0given to\u00a0debt financing and keeping reserves for more complicated scenarios, when the access to\u00a0debt financing is\u00a0even more difficult. Moreover, no\u00a0doubt that the available reserves serve as\u00a0an\u00a0insurance from the market point of\u00a0view and make the access to\u00a0debt financing somewhat easier.</p>\n<p>The deficit resources of\u00a0government support should be concentrated on\u00a0assistance to\u00a0the most vulnerable population groups, as\u00a0well as on\u00a0the development of\u00a0infrastructure and human capital.</p>\n\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-content -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"reply\"><a rel='nofollow' class='comment-reply-link' src='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/028c9ed93d3715863a09bb6a468f6cdf?s=60&#038;d=mm&#038;r=pg' srcset='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/028c9ed93d3715863a09bb6a468f6cdf?s=120&amp;d=mm&amp;r=pg 2x' class='avatar avatar-60 photo' height='60' width='60'/>\t\t\t\t\t\t<b class=\"fn\"><a href='http://Conspiracyofman.com' rel='external nofollow' class='url'>Arch Stanton</a></b> <span class=\"says\">says:</span>\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-author -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-metadata\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/who-is-to-blame-for-the-migrant-crisis-in-europe/#comment-948321\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<time datetime=\"2017-03-02T20:21:20+00:00\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tMarch 2, 2017 at 8:21 pm\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</time>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-metadata -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</footer><!-- .comment-meta -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p>While we&#8217;re addressing the thoughts of a Catholic Bishop, (one I find I am in agreement with on this subject as well as the hallowedhoax) yesterday was &#8220;Ash Wednesday,&#8221; yet another sick, twisted, insanely, bloody Old Testament <a Href=\"http://www.jewishencyclopedia.com/articles/1944-ashes\" rel=\"nofollow\">custom</a> adopted by &#8220;Judaeo-Christians&#8221; in the name of their mistaken savior. </p>\n<blockquote><p>In the Red Heifer ritual, for purification from defilement by contact with a corpse (Num. xix.), the Ashes of the offering are to be put into water, some of which is then to be sprinkled on the unclean person; their virtue is, of course, derived from the sacred material of the offering.&#8221;</p>\n<p>A mourner cast Ashes (or dust) on his head (II Sam. xiii. 9), or sat (Job ii. 8; Jonah iii. 6) or lay (Esth. iv. 3) or rolled himself (Jer. vi. 26; Ezek. xxvii. 30) in Ashes (or dust). The rendering &#8220;ashes&#8221; for the Hebrew word in question is, however, in some cases doubtful. In a number of passages in which it occurs <i>(in all, indeed, except those relating to the Red Heifer), it might as well or better be translated &#8220;dust&#8221;</i>; so where a person is said to eat, feed on, sit in, lie, or wallow in the &#8220;efer&#8221;; or put it on his head; or where it is used to represent finely attenuated matter (Ps. cxlvii. 16). Its use appears to be substantially identical with that of the word &#8220;&#8216;afar,&#8221; commonly rendered &#8220;dust.&#8221; The sense of humiliation is expressed by sitting or rolling in the &#8220;&#8216;afar&#8221; or dust (Isa. xlvii. 1; Micah i. 7, vii. 17; Ps. lxxii. 9); grief and suffering by putting dust on the head (Josh. vii. 6; Job ii. 12). The word symbolizes attenuation and annihilation or extinction (Job xxx. 19; Ps. xviii. 43 [42]); it is even employed to designate the burnt remains of the Red Heifer (Num. xix. 17).&#8221;</p></blockquote>\n<p>Note, all references to ashes come from the Old Testament. Where does Jesus or his apostles tell anyone to sprinkle ashes anywhere? The only place where ashes are actually specified in the above are in relation to the Red Heifer. </p>\n<p>These are the very special ashes of the Para Aduma&#8217;s ritual purification ceremony, the onerously expensive ashes of a ceremony that resulted in Jews entombing their loved ones alive in the sepulcher. This was the critical issue that set Jesus on the road to perdition with the Sanhedrin. </p>\n<p>While Christians pay lip service to Jesus, they actually practice Old Testament Judaism. Sprinkling ashes on one&#8217;s head is yet another sick, twisted Jewish ceremonial rite unwittingly adopted by the Chrsitian goyim masses; one totally antithetical to their savior&#8217;s words and deeds. </p>\n<p>In their Ash Wednesday ceremony, Christians <a Href=\"https://s-media-cache-ak0.pinimg.com/564x/48/a6/94/48a694461ce2ee4186befdc1dc1cf390.jpg\" rel=\"nofollow\">mark</a> the individual in the very same manner Jewish priests <a Href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=n7AIwvbyT5c\" rel=\"nofollow\">marked</a> their followers&#8217; sacrificial tribute, as depicted in this Jewish Hollywood movie. This is yet another bow to Judaic sacrificial tradition where Christians unwittingly celebrate the Jews&#8217; sacrificial murder of their savior. </p>\n<p>I don&#8217;t know how others might feel about Jesus, but frankly I see no reason to commemorate his grotesque murder. I would gladly accept my own sins if it meant  Jesus would not have had to suffer crucifixion. After all isn&#8217;t assuming responsibility for one&#8217;s own sins the very least one might do for such a great guy?  </p>\n<p>Ash Wednesday is but one modified Old Testament overlay that Jesus sought to remedy with his anti-Temple ministry. Another is modern Mormon&#8217;s invoking the underlying revenue demands of the second Temple priesthoods&#8217; ten percent tithing, a legal precedent established in the story of Abram&#8217;s sacrifice of  ten percent of his war booty to Melchizedek.   </p>\n<p>Another glaring example of the Christians&#8217; embrace of Old Testament custom is the celebration of the last supper. &#8220;Friday begins according to Jewish tradition, as, according to the three Synoptic Gospels, the Last Supper was held on the feast of Passover;[4] according to the Gospel of John, however, Jesus had his last supper on Nisan 14, the night before the first night of Passover.&#8221; </p>\n<p>Jesus&#8217; actions at the last supper, replayed at every communion, &#8220;Take this bread, this is my body&#8221; was a sarcastic mocking of the Temple&#8217;s sick sacrificial ceremony, whereby priests were allotted ten percent of the sacrifice for their own consumption. In contrast, the priests maintained their &#8220;Lord G_d&#8221; YHVH preferred only the fat and viscera of the animal burnt upon the sacrificial altar. </p>\n<p>Ya sure, you betcha! Ten percent of the prime cuts of the best animal for the priests and the remaining bloody guts for &#8220;Lord G_d&#8221; YHVH. Most telling of the depth of this religious lie was the full extent of the sacrificial blood lust, &#8220;Drink this wine, this is my blood&#8221; (the blood of a sacrificial paschal lamb).</p>\n<p>Drinking blood  is an act vehemently proscribed by Jewish law and custom. By this act, Jesus mocks the secret ceremony where Temple priests drank sacrificial blood in the privacy of the Tabernacle&#8217;s (and later the Temple&#8217;s) inner sanctum. </p>\n<p>Like his Essene brethren, Jesus was totally opposed to the Temple sacrifice. He repeatedly rejected the Temple&#8217;s requirement for sacrificial tribute. In fact, sacrificial tribute is the reason for his attack on the Temple moneylenders. Can there be any reason other than ridicule for Jesus&#8217; mock observance of an established, disgusting Jewish custom? . . . I&#8217;m listening. </p>\n<p>Modern Christians admonishing others to accept Jesus as their savior, are in fact unwittingly asking the unbeliever to accept the basic tenets of Judaism. Paradoxically, these are the very tenets that led to Jesus&#8217; crucifixion. Jesus tried hard to rectify these Jewish religious tenets by attacking the Temple&#8217;s laws and customs. </p>\n<p>Christians will exclaim &#8220;Yes! Jesus is our savior &#8211; but we must observe the ten commandments.&#8221; This demonstrates total ignorance of Jesus&#8217; two commandments that superseded not only those ten, but the original 633 commandments imposed by the Jewish Torah. </p>\n<p>If you love Jesus and truly believe he is your savior, then the greatest honor you can accord him is the full rejection of all of Judaism&#8217;s Old Testament laws and customs by religions that observe them in his name.   </p>\n<p>Jesus, what a guy! . . . What &#8211; a &#8211; Guy!!!</p>\n\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-content -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"reply\"><a rel='nofollow' class='comment-reply-link' paragraph we certainly agree on.</p>\n<p> \u201cIf you love Jesus and truly believe he is your savior, then the greatest honor you can accord him is the full rejection of all of Judaism\u2019s Old Testament laws and customs by religions that observe them in his name.\u201d</p>\n<p>To practice what Jesus taught, all the other deceptions have to be given up.  That is why when I am asked if I am a Christian, I say no and state that I am a follower of the teachings of Jesus.  Sometimes my reply leads to constructive discussions about the difference.  I certainly do not miss not going to \u201cchurch\u201d and silently disagreeing with the majority of what is spoken from the pulpit as they mostly avoid the Gospels while giving tremendous attention and credibility to the Old Testament and Acts through Revelations.  It appears that the biggest thing in the way of people not knowing the simplicity and empowerment of the teachings of Jesus is the confusion resulting from the doctrines of the \u201cchuches.\u201d</p>\n\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-content -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"reply\"><a rel='nofollow' class='comment-reply-link' href='https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/who-is-to-blame-for-the-migrant-crisis-in-europe/?replytocom=948343#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( \"div-comment-948343\", \"948343\", \"respond\", \"61261\" )' aria-label='Reply to Ungenius'>Reply</a></div>\t\t\t</article><!-- .comment-body -->\n<ol class=\"children\">\n\t\t<li id=\"comment-948378\" class=\"comment odd alt depth-3\">\n\t\t\t<article id=\"div-comment-948378\" class=\"comment-body\">\n\t\t\t\t<footer class=\"comment-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-author vcard\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<img alt='' src='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/028c9ed93d3715863a09bb6a468f6cdf?s=60&#038;d=mm&#038;r=pg' srcset='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/028c9ed93d3715863a09bb6a468f6cdf?s=120&amp;d=mm&amp;r=pg 2x' class='avatar avatar-60 photo' height='60' width='60'/>\t\t\t\t\t\t<b class=\"fn\"><a href='http://Conspiracyofman.com' rel='external nofollow' class='url'>Arch Stanton</a></b> <span class=\"says\">says:</span>\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-author -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-metadata\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/who-is-to-blame-for-the-migrant-crisis-in-europe/#comment-948378\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<time datetime=\"2017-03-03T18:12:04+00:00\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tMarch 3, 2017 at 6:12 pm\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</time>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-metadata -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</footer><!-- .comment-meta -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p>Jesus provided but a small window into the esoteric teachings of the masters.</p>\n<blockquote><p>All dervish teachers employ formulations through which to provide their teachings. Taken in isolation, as in the case of people examining things with insufficient information, these procedures, materials and ideas may seem to be associated with other creeds and with practices dating from immemorial time, or they may appear to areas which are not, strictly speaking, metaphysical. But since the basic knowledge of the dervishes is often not known to these observers, the reasons for Sufis choosing certain methods themselves remain equally unknown.</p></blockquote>\n<p>Under the doctrine of time, place and people, such teachers tailor their teachings specifically to function within these parameters. Thus their methods will not apply or function properly outside the doctrine&#8217;s parameters. </p>\n<p>This explains why many of Jesus&#8217; parables seem inexplicable to the modern mind. According to Sufi lore, most religious ceremonies and practices were, in their original form, concrete exercises necessary for the &#8220;work.&#8221; </p>\n<p>However, people intrigued and attracted by the outward mystical nature of these exercises adopted them and continued their practice without understanding the original purpose and nature of the practice. Thus these practices have come down through the ages as sacred ceremonies and observances with no other purpose then that of eliciting useless emotional states within the practitioner.</p>\n<blockquote><p>Because they never publicly adopted any distinctive dress, and because their members never carried on attention-attracting activities, scholars have not been able to reconstruct the history of the order. </p></blockquote>\n<p>While this statement relates to the Naqshbandi order, it applies equally well to the Essene order  that taught Jesus the esoteric knowledge. The Essene were Sufis before Sufis. The Essene order formed to accomplish a specific task, that of relieving Jews from their oppressive, false religion and its destructive practices.</p>\n<p>With the destruction of the Temple in 70 AD the Essene mission was complete and the order dissolved. Today little is know of their ancient structure. What remains are those who practice the remnant teachings of the order of which Jesus was a member. Thus, while the modern Essene provide valuable insight as to the original teachings of this order, they will never produce another Jesus.  </p>\n<p>The Sufis maintain that while religion is a &#8220;good start,&#8221; ultimately it must be transcended if one is to progress upon the path to enlightenment. While religion provides the basic structural outline of the esoteric teachings, primarily in its recognition of a higher form, commonly referred to as &#8220;god,&#8221; its emotionally based nature soon provides a barrier to one&#8217;s progress. Therefore one must move beyond religion if one is to find truth.</p>\n<p>One begins this process by reading, but then must practice the knowledge learned. Reading without practice is of no value. When one has properly applied themselves to these tasks, a teacher will find the seeker. Ultimately this is the direction undertaken by all human souls. Those mired in the material world will expend many lifetimes in the useless pursuit of this world. </p>\n<p>All true teachers eschew the destructive influence of the material world. Recognized teachers like Jesus and Buddha implored their followers to give up their worldly desires and wealth to pursue that which is of real value to the soul&#8217;s progress. The pursuits and desires of the material world all eventually fade into nothingness, only the soul is immortal.   </p>\n<p>The path to enlightenment is the most difficult of all human undertakings. The highest level of standard education is but mere preschool primer by comparison. Unlike standard education, the path takes many lifetimes to complete.  As Lao-tzu said: &#8220;A journey of a thousand miles begins with a single step.&#8221; The spiritual journey of the soul is infinitely longer than any physical journey.
